In many cases, if you acquire a majority of the voting stock, you can replace the board quickly and with a few formalities, but other companies are <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/w1MHuR7XINEcJopl1QHQUXqkDuummxjK1qdBoKDskxHMk\_oTkHC5u5HarsORMMp7oA7B8hZfWsNrYwbracXG3tcqmZPArR9xowb9GSAmUuyK0hbvkWy4UrGLwPpN8isoo9B3TvCXpVvSxxLQ9pFVmOqD7xVyLzGOD7sFGlXeMSm0P8rrRdejyABBJ7pj2cZLUzsJyEKNrrOqvzX4tyFaVpuhvvq-Ui-sHtvXzS2nS68N79EvlFbQtoVLLhEN0qmCqBnJlO\_pqGSOKdWYaAkv6-LoenBdaVWCQedqUIF8iTkxMcgukEOvf16aXxkVLyQfB26-qC9fGPUt\_ZA57HnrGriJmfgRKGexKqsb1jAsId\_5ot7dUtw45ZCfmHo/qw8EMPoLrjyJfiNNkOWbd0Qd4G7ninrk/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">structured in such a way</a> that it could take years even if you have a majority of the stock.</p> </div> <div id="footnote-2" style="font-style: italic;"> <p style="margin: 16px 0;">[2] During this limbo, in 2024, someone <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/6RXJFTVT0Q11lKPz88JahXVO5NTN1X1pCOKVoohMv3KXw6rvCFyqlhP-ZP4IXJWyJwqmQ-\_Su63o0bl7aAW8EaA2GbHPvFDwZSXKxn1y1YQSMUc7\_bdOJHsHx9hpkgIrRkSAOWhTYybxmBm3sUlIG5UYUQdvA0Xi0-RbT2YvHhXWuL3oNi079voLmzk8ENpMduJZMtG3GiXDyiWFm9quto2CLvr5fsMx0AD0F4nkXq-jFC8pClO4BAPoXa2OuEcnVn4FtejkMLj13RicXOuJ743Tl1ZkvdBvLYIhx69RTGaHSUxU6q1goY7HcAgC5Vyb44i7VbKMw18D1HKWR8f0tnTACPmsk2lxe1NBMCuUFnOE\_zwuLGplj4FUdJY/Og1tOF0tAhFxC148gjYQF3Jy9EXfpU\_g/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">launched a mini-tender</a> at $0.03 per share. A <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/QdQb5uWYwyrjiAr\_yr9AgA7UjWt3D9YZywW\_fFYJkiCvVVit24PE54rk2Ii6e0mWSuJuIWA4SRrF9c18nVz6DywLO68kHo1d0BqayFJcF8ZObYk556OCkytpEdKpzs6UJeoFa\_JpvjDEHX4UZClqSXA5vVcBzVZG0--r3Og8y-74qFCQc\_waPJ3iOKf-QnBqDQV26nmynkCM7L\_1MU-IKjSsyKpV2aYFyK\_PtVBYPjnNDo3OgTOnFw6e0QFn5mDKdhFP\_5MRYHD9atH0cF03nLwJimTyjro0pSMtFxRpkwNbQp7Y9kNnLc0uG0V9PJxGqc7\_H8G94EXXh\_4cJ3qNqR8ruNK962\_h9PcV77KNPYvcXvOXw0Kju-0\_8uU/iyrynQ3xJ29P1QiTOeiM9ulQ8FPV-J6d/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">mini-tender</a> is a sort of mild scam in which an interloper offers to buy a bunch of shares at way below their market price; confused or careless shareholders sometimes tender without realizing that they’re getting underpaid. Here, getting $0.03 after the stock hadn’t traded for five years might have seemed appealing, though the board (correctly!) recommended that shareholders not tender, given, you know, all the cash.</p> </div> <div id="footnote-3" style="font-style: italic;"> <p style="margin: 16px 0;">[3] From the opinion: “Just as shareholder democracy is fortified by the requirement that shareholders must be notified in advance of an AGM of any special business, so it is an important aspect of shareholder democracy that shareholders retain the freedom to elect whom they choose as directors at an AGM, without that being subject to a requirement for prior notice. Section 109 places the duty to give notice of special business upon the company, in the notice convening the AGM. The exclusion of the election of directors from special business ensures that the shareholders retain dominion over who the directors should be, without interference from the company, at the direction of the current board.”</p> </div> <div id="footnote-4" style="font-style: italic;"> <p style="margin: 16px 0;">[4] That is, $55 times 71.8 million, which is <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/WLCYb7OebpBRzx\_oOm4b3UoaX0Yt-ahX2qZ7m8vpeUbN1TsFW0EzVdeS8bAQkQorIEszoHUN3VszIguYDLCrypHjguwBqqxbjfzd2he8LSs8d2bZ6mac9uERAjFdWkS87bOi1KIe4cH9o1sGOVlnA60YbCF3aNdeUZgolgE6A2dDlQDdQa4-2czII8CseZruj5-yg7kDtPGrm\_royI53Pz0luqYI9eANzYGjbA9cW-zhB7Ae3t9vIKNmPJi0Ty21pJJ1sA0JyB8DqWTE6NyemCmM-xjBzYEgc4hyLBLjdGaGnrcftuifaNjaMiH2SDnTZS60njA\_FY3OSTQcKL84ENA0myn9ALCZJWWOAQQBwoCosDsf8QGNrTzW-r0/zspzOn6jTmQslUyoh8ak5zOVX2u0S9pX/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">one guess</a> at the number of outstanding shares. The <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/16-yTDdtpqnK0VfMoMSLZ6vfMMfOb0JHyNWvFBI0jVKqE96YyXF5ktScFUqcoXWoUAAqnce5TacotyQz5cTxyp\_dFEKfcz38elzOTFMlw5fpNVDKrBp9pUjGN4eZA55uuIK-9PRcHhdDcO8BbzqHufFXp5-dt2BhYIpgX12rHyPag5dETaklV-l0WtCQZWF3qgVztatdagyufLaw2qaL55hiv9FvKS-MNUSLzR0Elvr3g\_WHr4KYLEBnUiqFNgvHKLD72ZHC1fz\_rxHR6htMQxSM6st0UeOwpBJat6uiUEZ7D\_zjPTBlSg\_2qbFjtAECj7tVKnQAyNYjO4PjP6jSdVr0\_FxuJvBrPLwdf3-vdBEm-Czjh6F4yOWVwI0/QuQdWREna6HH1pZlGxpPJDYggygYYx2R/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">press release notes</a> that 11.8 million of those shares were issued by the imposter board in a 2018 PIPE, the new board is still pondering those, and “an amount equal to the aggregate amount of cash that would be payable under the Dividend in respect of the 2018 PIPE Shares, will, prior to the payment date, be set aside and retained by the Company pending final resolution of any issues with respect to the 2018 PIPE Shares based on the Board’s assessment in accordance with the Order and under the laws of Antigua and Barbuda.” So could be more like $3.3 billion.</p> </div> <div id="footnote-5" style="font-style: italic;"> <p style="margin: 16px 0;">[5] Also, I <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/XVBP5yOtlBkHt6XIqwCJ6J2IcuzZoMqqvDn162tNh43vIs1ZUkZXEbKySCk-zkH0te65rRfrtdY0IUg77BaDUGBU7fr36RsQ94wzlIPpxnJXaYk4aXBCia5ZB-v6j6Qn9lrJtLQyL0jM\_ROe58dSc3\_XXvtrLO8kaG9UWAB-19tStFYidx\_qiQsEYJ\_mvFmAYKflt4OJH7oOlzou-n3GZGIu6Xp8e0qvV28wLbovGwL-Ul1ggbvgUoaFg26xYnUWexeIaNO\_t-dHsEPH\_4wi5pQU7YhjuvOQu8c7XfY0k7echA3ozGVnMyFo29HwFQ6De37q6plxEVOP2BAObp3uHJz85cOqp9e4u8O0ec\_c3aLfCKw0YKaaceStAGo/QyC2H4obkdQ3ZTyhdOPiyCZeN3cU\_pc9/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">sometimes</a> say <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/ApAwIsWRuo6zePctEc0OIVLD3GrH2A48nJ45jvFsg3mB1oOvx\_Jpw1n4ZG\_WBIfmdJ6LgzeS7xd37NtimfeQk-e04lcTMFr01zsf3L3BYwWY\_pkjCdkWKAocbpCmyC6ZJTAYeGbGfPqUIrANHi0deK-9vD8aN47NasmGD85yReRYbheRPKTcsc9JfolFqCPWEWVtKXhiBCYnkZbiYiWBN6Bm5aCMDqxkISqdMnBYVQoUAmt8Yqx3loaNaUH\_2g9tXgfX1NOygib8WcVcPZeG83dbHbL1HQmgOlCusHTBB1R9ex9mrZT-gWSlgmhAzAV1Z8IOlZpP\_24LJcfKXfJ79F0LYzTlxUZZlNynpIbgkWJaEt3bRHTx3c1hqMo/SAnpi4DCTjegUo\_a4Zx2ofQ3LO3qeDTQ/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">that</a> the practical answer to “who controls the company” is something like “whoever has the keys to the office and the passwords to the website.” We have discussed a company that filed dueling 8-Ks, where both sides sequentially had access to the company’s SEC filing keys. Something like that happened here: On July 9, the 1Globe/OrbiMed board <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/h0vcRPlGQogHQn0irtes8zjOURtZTYJ4Eoe4XWSilQGv2xLd3HXm3doV6Scfl67JAi\_Q8odXyAd4w0J2XqK2Z3u5bv\_A74J5lXskRHrOwKdW6IKudbYgY0eWrn8el-McTEWBurrFNO7KZYL8eQHD7gzMknlhrJQh3aTegWZaklZ8c53PaOWUQVy7G-\_gBWrw5zH3jO0rNix9lr\_6KLqzsEpOcDl1M7NJRNSDrIrJaijXHZ-7TzgljP9FVBZ\_XI-j5LHyLcc30QzBn0jpQpwjzKLSJTmxMF5LVrOUF3lpvKn7od6MR8ePRuaiRgiWv-F62feAiS0-F9IQAHjluO10bAfegC1mekURiRymMK6oRJpVHPfrB-fTspRQvYE/k0euQ9Uk5c2BvZRCaabvMKOW2QJeaY8Q/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">filed</a> its announcement that the SAIF/Vivo board were imposters (again); on July 10, though, the SAIF/Vivo board <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/0Yzi4hQwIvfsWIf\_xKdJ\_Gc6M1vZfNuUImnKZH6uOhMf1dNYJHYLjvCi68Q5F43iNFOSzchKbpbnHF6KzzdtEgVEjLjBXpxPMdEe51tHz\_ZB9BsnJAzqIYA8IY3-tQdhPRCFs9HFe-ju4KN0lIgRwFVuXUfsZM7izJRM9ToAFHvUvcy2PBFTSE3ZMrJ4i7YpMhyIky9CuF0ODd9MwvMvO\_cHHoXReoOkzxWt5q8zdUx\_6GUGkotho\_KWfOKEZg961qYxhgyBZ3HzR\_HRaa8T4DwoHlqqqliL9VSaS5fbcFYyi6DvO1\_SsY9qqtQAgAPf4enyz0jyH0iV6pJS8xhcI3J5NrypA\_TSm4mfhEc677jlNRAdRnZEZf6IPYg/eHHlWUz5R2E\_wWwSLkId-rQBXvSCdn\_N/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">filed</a> its announcement that it’s the board now. Both announcements were signed by the chairman of the board, though, different chairmen. The SAIF/Vivo <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/Sj992Sa0-f6LoCVZujXSg8xU2CUyLpJ39--6XR3ND5vjW2kUl8haYdDwJWcGTA292KFpc7et2V0GEoltI8XtAeHRxlbI2BX90kiAkI3MQpWnDHVe\_yZzu8Dl4zv7BV1y4twrzkS8PzrRDSFNEbzgYBDrapbETR98chXVp7qdtkHB7o7tqOiXlP4-MBHiGPtUMiNDMOhlrz\_FtKFxoRiU0chrfZxKd19GJwnd2\_cn2oKVsgDj5ttAMXxzIWARcp3cqtsK\_73wN-87pU8w47MVJUB6CY0mqW-QdjezFvqaLoNRggDG7eAFqc13a7INayCpz3Npis6dIDqvp8EbaIZDoBbAnmeHf342so\_r9ndzUu1RdZA0hnCs52piQ6U/oUdOoAzBSOApWnb9VqOmRcSC4aezTAsK/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">announcement</a> “confirmed that Mr. Yin Weidong shall continue to serve as Executive Director and Chief Executive Officer of the Company,” so maybe he’s reporting to them now. Maybe he has the passwords?</p> </div> <div id="footnote-6" style="font-style: italic;"> <p style="margin: 16px 0;">[6] And besides the <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/H0j8nMG\_IOffPZ-zZAWhf6eLHsrAKGedQNoFLyJpqrTfNhOiPhZCDFuWy-bx2rrUvAvXqFUhd6cC2ba9e0xI6C53vu0cXO-jusV9XeJfj2wcbFEi5sG225lg-REF84ESVbG51v0D\_qxb5jiRR1KHP-sS11RHT-37mSCk-KClEsfLCgPEXepwCYE4rxrfPmwbBy-l3lIZDQ8M6oG8nDikEkx4D-RfICAqU8O2UMjBR0kOBh6Yt5FyEsYDgdpGrWBucR95NIj5v8elKsUg4u\_MFUJSx1cmPM60UP33NNNkYxr1olo5ICzbSdVIAQjPS2pv2-bmEBcxNfn5NHQ22aMXNAkaZIjIcG71uEqJF8WqrtnGBS2HWyhD8Atd1MQ/D3MxqXu\_cbaDCEtVzy2Vy7dC5-qU94yu/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank">standard sort</a> of social-issue <a href="https://links.message.bloomberg.com/s/c/Km7JoTXWe7rU7yYgRaO0mWgGK-x5Tz3lrSisrPt3QlPTKYpGH4YPojlRdQyHGNlmd3HF\_6ziDMwgIgx1NJj2KRSYCoEeLyUDwpwIxDS8cJdfwD01tU3r1vJG-gDcOG90DFEtRPop7YuXpTKMIWrDM9ECpK1WzsEkZ5dAmUmQFRdRspEpZt\_3nOVh-Wfx966glqawUKrJ3BYVUdYLULh\_6hB76pfQoD99BBsf-4htx4PO-qTSgJhrMmJBa7Aw0OqMr7ClT2TLyoc3dLg2rUru86Wrj6T2uXe2bFdqeZcpKhYi4oWgyqOqHGP1kSpfiBwuLj4Ei7Dd7yfZ0NJxqUqBMzBv7Wxg6UTk8RgYeEHLpevopMn9PVyyeYjhY5k/VuK8j6Y8sKNoz5I53iQNuIzGN6O5aDf7/11" itemprop="StoryLink" itemscope="itemscope" style="color: #000000; text-decoration: none !important; border-bottom-width: 1px; border-bottom-color: #000000; border-bottom-style: solid; background-color: #ccc;" target="\_blank"> 14a-8</a> activists. I mean people agitating for strategic shifts or new management.</p> </div> </td> </tr> </table> </td> </tr> <tr> <td style="border-collapse: collapse; mso-table-lspace: 0pt; mso-table-rspace: 0pt;
